		picture = gtfo
		potential = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					is_culture_group = germanic
					OR = {
						AND = { owns = 736 NOT = { has_global_flag = germanic_renamed_trieste } }
						AND = { owns = 3642 NOT = { has_global_flag = germanic_renamed_gradisca } }
						AND = { owns = 737 NOT = { has_global_flag = germanic_renamed_gorz } }
						AND = { owns = 3641 NOT = { has_global_flag = germanic_renamed_koper } }
						AND = { owns = 770 NOT = { has_global_flag = germanic_renamed_istria } }
						AND = { owns = 778 NOT = { has_global_flag = germanic_renamed_fiume } }

				limit = {
					province_id = 17
					owner = {
						OR = {
							tag = ENG
							tag = ENL
							tag = CAN
							tag = RPL
							AND = {
								tag = COL
								NOT = { primary_culture = cascadian }
							}
							AND = {
								is_culture_group = american_cultures
								NOT = {
									OR = {
										tag = CAS
										tag = UOR
										tag = JEF
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				# 21 = { change_province_name = "Kootenay" }
				17 = { change_province_name = "Stikine" }
				owner = { 
					set_global_flag = anglo_rename_stickine
					clr_global_flag = CAS_rename_stickine
					clr_global_flag = slavic_rename_stickine
					clr_global_flag = spic_rename_stickine
